        let oInsights = window.oVa.insights ? window.oVa.insights : {}

        if(oRemoveAds.indexOf('trb_ad_1280x220/970x250/970x90/728x90/320x100/320x50_1_/') != -1 && true) {

            let params = {
              id: 'hp_1794',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.mcall/hp',
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true
            }

              trb.data.page.ads.vendor = trb.data.page.ads.vendor || {}
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams = trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams || {}
            }
            const dimensions = !' [[[1280, 220], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [320, 100], [320, 50]]] '.length ? null : JSON.parse(' [[[1280, 220], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [320, 100], [320, 50]]] '),
              sizemapDimensions = !'[[1280, 0], [800, 0], [0, 0]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[1280, 0], [800, 0], [0, 0]]')
            if (sizemapDimensions) {
              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1794'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1794'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }

          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_1280x220/970x250/970x90/728x90/320x100/320x50_1_/");

              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_1280x220/970x250/970x90/728x90/320x100/320x50_1_/', true);
              }
            }

              id: 'hp_1794',

               <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md hddn-dktp hddn-tbl hddn-mble" data-pb-field="description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">
                You might have more luck on your side depending on where you live, according to a new study. To determine which states were the most and least lucky in America, career site Zippia examined two key factors: health and finance. Each state was ranked based on factors such as number of Powerball and Jackpot lottery winners, median household income, unemployment, average life expectancy, weather fatalities and accidental car deaths per 100,000 people. Here are the 10 most and the 10 least lucky states in America, starting with the luckiest.

          label && label.classList.add('hddn')
          adFlag = false

            if (sizemapDimensions) {

              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_517'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)

              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_517'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)

The county is poised to join a small handful of municipalities across the nation using the burgeoning, and sometimes controversial, science of predictive analytics to decide which children are at risk.
